 During this time also, Captain Rohan made no attempt to pacify both
 kuch der baad priyanka mona ko apane paale main karti najar ai
 After this, 'bigg Boss' summoned Rohan to the confession room and asked how his captaincy was going
 tab rohan ne kaha ki vah puri koshish kar rahe hai lekin 'big bos' behatar bataa paaenge
 Bigg Boss then said that his captaincy had become a joke
 is par rohan ne kaha ki koi unki baat nahin sunata or unhen lagata he ki captain ke paas or adhik adhikaar hone chahie
 On this, 'bigg Boss' said- 'can't be mean?' When Rohan again repeated that no one listened to him
 is par 'big bos' ne unhen torget karte hue kaha, 'sach kah rahe hai, agar koi sunanaa hi nahin chahta he to use lakh samajhane kii koshish bhi kam he
 ' kuch der baad bani or sahil is baat par charchaa karne lage ki khaanaa kaaphi der se ban rahaa he
 Bani said that earlier there was a time table of everything
 ab safai bhi nahin ho rahi he, bathroom bahut gande hai
 Bani said that it is the captain's job to assign work to the householders
 iske kuch der baad gharavaalon ko bulaakar 'big bos' ne kaha
 'it is a matter of pride to be the captain of any team, more than that, the responsibilities are increased, along with the responsibilities, the rights are also increased
 lekin jab ghar ke captain ko unki laaparvaahee kii taraf dhyaan dilaayaa jaataa he to vah kehete hai ki unhen or adhikaar chahie or koi baat nahin sunata to vah kya kar sakate hai
 Perhaps no householder considers him worthy of a captain
 'big bos' ko yah kehane main jaraa bhi khed nahin he ki captain ke taur par rohan puri tarah se asafal hue hai
 After this, 'bigg Boss' took away Rohan's captaincy and announced that he will never be able to become captain now in the entire season
 big bos ke is faisle se rohan chidh gaye or gharavaalon se poochne lage ki jis kisi ko lagata he ki vah captain ke taur par fail hue hai vah apana haath uthaae, phir vah kehane lage ki dekhte hai aglaa captain kya karata he
 He also objected that he would no longer be named captain
 lopamudra ne unhen santvanaa dene kii koshish kii ki unka kaam acha tha
 Meanwhile, Manu and Monalisa were seen talking on the next captaincy while Swami Om said that Rohan was proud and that it was good that 'bigg Boss' removed him
 tippaniyan During this, Manu and Mona were talking about captaincy in the garden area of the house
 bedroom main baithi nitibha kii taraf ishaara karte hue manu punjabi ne kaha ki dekho manavir ke saath ek hi razaai main ghuskar baithi he
 Manu said that he does not understand anything of Nitibha that the distance remains throughout the day and comes in the evening and sticks with them
 raat 12 baje bani kaa janmdin celibratt karne ke baad gharavaalon kaa din khatm hua
 After this, 'bigg Boss' called Rohan to the confession room and asked him whether he understood the responsibility he was assigned to send the nominated members to the Challenger room
 On this, Rohan said that he tried his best but nobody listened to him
 is par 'big bos' ne kaha ki unhen adhik form rahakar apni baat manavaani padegi
 After this, Manveer and Manu saw Swami Om hiding something in his pillow
 unhone jaakar check kiya to dekha ki manu or swami om ke takie main chammachein rakhi hui thim
 When Swami Om was asked why he did this, he said that iron protects him from demonic powers, so he did it
 haalanki unhone safai di ki unhone manu ke takie main saamaan nahin daalaa he
 After this, Manveer, Priyanka and Manu searched Swami Om's mattress and belongings
 swami om ke bag main se ghar waalon ke shampoo, condishnar, dio or kai chijen nikaleen
 On this, Swami said that he had kept all the things for the family only that they would use when it was over
 vah is baat ke liye manu or manavir par chillane lage ki unhone unki anupasthiti main unka saamaan churaayaa he
 Swami Om and Manveer debated fiercely about this, even during this, Captain Rohan kept watching silently
 kuch der baad swami om jab rone lage to manavir, manu or nitibha ne unhen shant karaayaa ki takie se chammach niklaa isliye sab gusse main aa gaye the
 Manveer said that if there are four people in the house, then there will be a fight
 iske kuch der baad swami om manavir ko bataate dikhe ki unka ek kurta chori ho gaya he, is par manavir ne kaha ki unhen sara saamaan mil jayega
 After this Swami started telling Om Priyanka that Manu and Manveer lie against each other
 is par priyanka ne kaha ki baahar jaaenge tab sab pataa chalegaa
 Mona overhears both of them and forbids them to do evil to Manu and Manveer
 iske kuch der baad kichan aria main priyanka or monalisa ke bich jamkar bahes ho gai
 Monalisa tells Priyanka that she is no one to tell them their limits, Manu defends the middle then both of them quarrel
 is dauraan bhi captain rohan ne donon ko shant karaane kii koi koshish nahin kii
 After some time Priyanka was seen doing Mona in her court
 iske baad 'big bos' ne rohan ko canfeshan room main bulaakar poocha ki unki captaini kisi chal rahi he
 Then Rohan said that he is trying his best but 'bigg Boss' will be able to tell better
 tab 'big bos' ne kaha ki unki captaini majaak ban chuki he
 On this, Rohan said that no one listens to him and he feels that the captain should have more powers
 is par 'big bos' ne kaha- 'matlab ho nahin paa rahaa he?' is par jab rohan ne phir doharaaya ki koi unki baat nahin sunata he
 On this, 'bigg Boss' targeted him and said,' Telling the truth, if someone does not want to listen, then there is less effort to convince him
 ' After some time, Bani and Sahil started discussing that the food was being made quite late
 bani ne bataaya ki pehle ek time teble hota tha sab cheez kaa
 Cleaning is no longer happening, bathrooms are very dirty
 bani ne kaha ki gharavaalon ko kaam asin karnaa captain kaa kaam he
 Shortly after this, 'bigg Boss' called the family members
 'kisi bhi team kaa captain bananaa garv kii baat he, usase badi baat jimmedaariyon ko nibhaana, jimmedaariyon ko nibhaane ke saath-saath adhikaar bhi bad jate hai
 But when the captain of the house is reminded of his negligence, he says that he needs more rights and he cannot listen to what he can do
 shaayad koi bhi gharavaala unhen captain ke laayak nahin samajhataa
 'bigg Boss' has no regrets in saying that Rohan as captain has completely failed
 ' iske baad 'big bos' ne rohan kii captaini chin lee or elaan kiya ki puure sijan main ab vah kabhi captain nahin ban paaenge

 iske baad manavir or manu ne swami om ko apane takiye main kuch chhipate dekha

 There are reports of collision between two trains at Kasara Ghat near Nashik in Maharashtra
 jaankaree ke anusaar ambareli or kasaara stesan ke bich vidarbha express ne ek local train ko takkar maar di
 Helpline number of Mumbai CST: 022-22694040 Hades night 9
 30 baje ke aas-paas hua
 According to the information received so far, 3 people have died in this accident while more than 31 people are reported injured
 raahat evam bachaav dal ko ghatnasthal ke liye ravaanaa kar diya gaya he

 aise main duusari ore se aa rahi vidarbha express bogiyon se takaraa gai
 Central Railway sources said that the accident occurred when some coaches of the mumbai-kasara local train derailed at around 9
30 pm and collided with the express train
 netaji subhash chandra bose ke naayab or pandit jawaharlal nehru ke 'puraane dost' asien nambiar soviet sangh ke jasoos the
 This has been claimed in British documents
 britain ke rashtriya abhilekhaagaar ke jo gopneey dastavej saarvajanik kiye gaye hai
 According to him, Nambiar went to Berlin in 1924 as a journalist and worked closely with the Communist Group of India
 vah 1929 main soviet ke 'mehmaan' ke rup main moscow gaye the
 Documents state that Nambiar was deported from Germany after World War II began, but he was later approved of Bose's arrival in Berlin as Nayab
 iske baad jab bose japan ke saath judane ke liye germany se sudur purv gaye to nambiar ko europe main aaazaad hind fouj ke vittiya netaa (german) kii jimmedaari saunpi gai
 According to the statement issued by the archives, Nambiar was also related to the Indian military group consisting of Indian pows, which was annexed by the Soviet Union in 1944
 nambiar ko june, 1945 main austria main giraftaar kiya gaya or naajiyon se santhganth ke taur par poochtacha kii gai thi
 After World War II, Nambiar started working as a consulate and Indian ambassador in Scandinavia in the Indian Mission in Bern, Switzerland and later moved to West Germany
 iske baad unhone 'hindustan times' ke europea samvaadadaata ke rup main kaam kiya
 The documents claimed that Nambiar was deployed to cover industrial intelligence activities
 british dastavejon main europe or germany main netaji kii aaazaad hind se sambandhit gatividhiyon ke naam evam vivaran shaamil hai
 The documents also contain copies of letters that Nambiar wrote to Bose
 ye patr germany kii pandubbi you-boat 234 se baraamad kiye gaye the
 Today is the birth anniversary of Mother Teresi
 unka janm 26 agast 1910 ko albeniai parivaar main hua tha
 His real name was Agnes Gonzha Boyajiju
 kusht rogiyon or anathon kii seva main apni jindagi lagane valimdar terresaconobelshanti puraskaar se sammanit kiya gaya he
 There will be someone in the world and especially in the Indian subcontinent who is not aware of the name and act of Mother Teresa

 Usually, we do not take the walls of the house in the house seriously, but after knowing this, any type of dampness present in the house can lead to serious respiratory diseases
 koi bhi apane ghar main pani ke risaav or usase hone vaali sillen ko kabhi panpane nahin dena chahega
 Whether the house is new or old, it is necessary to protect it from dampness and for this it is mandatory to do waterproofing
 isse sabhi prakaar kii sillen se bachaa ja saktaa he or saath hi bachaa ja saktaa he asthma jaisi shwaas sambandhi gambheer beemaari se, jiske bare main kaha jaataa he ki yah jaan lene ke saath hi sharir se jaati he
 So how to protect your home from water leakage or damping? According to Sanjay Bahadur, Global CEO (construction Chemical Division) of Pidilite Industries Limited, this problem can be overcome through waterproofing but to date, waterproofing should be seen as an investment and not a cost
 waterprufing kyon jaruri he? bakaul sanjay, kisi bhi nirmaan sataha par pani kaa aana daraar jaise muddon kaa kaaran banataa he, jo lambey samay tak ghar kii kshati kaa kaaran ban saktaa he
 Likewise, moisture on the walls contributes to mold growth, one of the many reasons that lead to respiratory diseases such as asthma

 waterprufing kahaan kii jaae?kuch nae gharon main basic waterprufing kii jaati he, lekin yah sirf chhaton tak simit hoti he
 But to make your home a 5-point leak-free home, it is necessary to have waterproofing done in all parts of the house from where there is a possibility of water intrusion
 hyae 5-point li-free home kaa arth he ki sirf chat par hi waterprufing nahin ho, balki andruni geele hisson jaise bathroom, kichan or balkani, bahari deevaaron, kancreet water tanks or tal ke nichle hisse main bhi waterprufing karai jaae

 ghar puri tarah se sangrakshit tabhi hoga jab sabhi paanch sambhav jal pravesh kshetron main thik se waterprufing karai jaae
 These five surfaces are important and there are some reasons, which are as follows - 1
 jameen ke neeche - sataha kaa pani samay kii avadhi main badhata jaataa he or aapke ghar main pravesh kar saktaa he, yah aantarik deevaaron ko nuksaan pahunchaata he
 2
 aantarik geele kshetra (snanaghar, rasoi or balakani) - ye kshetra 365 dinon tak yani lagaataar pani ke sampark main aate hai, jisase aantarik deevaaron par paint kharaab ho jaataa he or papadi dene lagata he
 3
 chat - taapmaana main hone vaale parivartan ke saath hi chat kii sataha main bhi badlaav hota he, jisase aapaki sundar chat par pani kaa risaav hone lagata he or isse puure ghar main nami aati he
 4
 kancreet water tanks - daraaron ke gathan ke kaaran ye pani ke tanks sataha ke madhyam se risaav kaa kaaran banate hai
 Therefore it is important to waterproof the area properly
 5
 Exterior Walls - Due to change in temperature, cracks are created in the external walls, due to which moisture starts coming and hence the look of your house also starts deteriorating

 jab bhi ham bollywood film industry main diggaj singrs kaa zikr karte hai kumaar sanu kaa naam hameshaa liya jaataa he
 In the 90s, Kumar Sanu led the film industry
 udit narayan or abhijit jaise diggaj gayakon ke hone ke baavjood kumaar sanu 90 ke dashak main sabase zyada sune jane vaale singer rahe
 Even today, whenever walking or traveling on the road, the melodious voice of Kumar Sanu is heard in the ears; kumaar sanu kaa janm 23 sitambar, 1957 main kolkata main hua
 Kumar Sanu's father Pashupati Bhattacharya was also a singer and musician
 jis samay kumaar sanu ne industry main entry maari thi us samay logon par kishor kumaar kaa jaadu tha
 But after the sudden demise of Kishore Kumar, a big place in the music world was vacant
 log kishor ke gane sunne ke aadi ho gaye the or logon ke bich unki jabardast fain folowing the
 In such a situation, Kumar Sanu filled the place with his voice and became a favorite of people on seeing it
 kumaar sanu ke janmdin ke maukey par sunen unke superhit gane
 This song from the film Mera Dil Bhi Pyaas Haisajan was sung by Kumar Sanu with Alka Yagnik
 ye apane samay kaa sabase superhit gaanaa he
 It remains in the favorite list of Song Couples
 ek ladki ko dekha to aisa laga-anil kapur kii film 1942 a lav story kaa ye gaanaa behad popular hua
 Javed Akhtar composed the lyrics and music was given by RD Burman
 vaise to is film ke saare gane kaaphi superhit the magar is gane kii baat hi kuch or he
 Even after two decades, this song seems to be always fresh
 dhire dhire pyaar ko badhanaa he-phool or kaante film kaa ye gaanaa bhi kamaal kaa he or kumaar sanu or alka yagnik kii aawaaj main ye gaanaa or bhi surmai lagata he
 Slowly come into my life - Whenever there is talk of Aashiqui film, this song is definitely a thing
 is film ke saare gane superhit the or inhen gaakar kumaar sanu bhi superhit ho gaye the
 The song was sung by Kumar Sanu with Anuradha Podwal
 dard karaara-kumaar sanu kaa jaadu lambey vakt ke baad ayushmaan khurana kii film dam laga ke haisha main dikhaa
 He sang Dard Karara Song
 'detective byomakesh bakshi'kaa nayaa gaanaa 'batch ke bakshi' relies ho gaya he
 Sushant is seen performing hip hop dance in this song
 is gane ke bol hai, 'batch ke bakshi tu jhootha he makkaar'
 The song has been shot on the film's lead actor Sushant Rajput
 ismensushantshandaar energetic dance muves karte najar aa rahe hai
 In the film, scenes filmed by Byomkesh Bakhshipar have been given the appearance of dance in this song
 yahi wo cheez he jo is gane ke khaas banaati he
 This special video of the song has been choreographed by dance choreographer Lauren Gottlieb
 3 april ko relies hone ja rahi is film kodibakar bannerjeene diarect kiya he
